Cycling</h2>\n                            <p>\n\tWe’re an independent, family-run chain of cycle shops, based in central England. Established in 1981, we now have 10 shops, including Britain’s biggest bike shop at Whitwell, Rutland Water; two Giant brand stores; and more shops at Grafham Water, Fineshade Wood, Peterborough and Cambridge. We’re proud to have won many industry awards, including the Family Business Award for Retail Excellence (2015), and Best Independent Cycling Retailer (2014, 2013, 2011, 2010).</p>\n<p>\n\tIn addition to stocking all the best bike brands, including Giant, Liv, Specialized, Trek, SCOTT, Cube, Cannondale, Santa Cruz, Bianchi, Whyte and Brompton, we also offer traffic-free cycle hire, a full workshop, Body Geometry Bike Fit, custom build, and a regular calendar of free rides and seminars.</p>\n<p>\n\tWe offer free standard delivery, 0% finance, Cycle to Work, and free enrolment to our Rutland Rewards scheme, where you can earn points on every purchase and redeem them online and in store.</p>\n<p>\n\tVisit us in store, buy online or use our free Click &amp; Collect service – we look forward to welcoming you.</p>\n<p>\n\tEnjoy the ride!</p>\n\n                        </div>\n                        <div class=\"col-75p\">\n                            <div class=\"col-2 ctrPad32 blogRightRecent\">\n                                <h2>Blog</h2>\n                                <p>The latest articles from the Rutland Cycling blog. Women’s bikes (sometimes described as “Women-Specific Design or “WSD”) bikes offer an alternative to a unisex or men’s bike, which is designed to better fit a woman’s frame and body shape. For example, the frame geometry may feature a shorter reach to the handlebars, as women’s arms and upper bodies tend to<a href=\"/content/women-s-cycling-guide.aspx\" onclick=\"ga('send', 'event',  'Homepage' , 'Click', '/content/women-s-cycling-guide.aspx', {'nonInteraction': 1})\">.... More </a></span>\n            <a href=\"/content/women-s-cycling-guide.aspx\" class=\"bBottom4\" onclick=\"ga('send', 'event',  'Homepage' , 'Click', '/content/women-s-cycling-guide.aspx', {'nonInteraction': 1})\"><span class=\"fa\"></span> Women’s Cycling Guide</a>\n        </div>\n    \n\n                                </div>\n                                <a href=\"/blog/blog.aspx\" class=\"button bSquare btn-thin-border\">Read The Blog</a>\n                            </div>\n                            <div class=\"col-2 ctrPad32 blogRightRecent\">\n                                <h2>Guides</h2>\n                                <p>Top tips to help you choose the best bike for your needs and allow you get the most from cycling.</p>\n                                <div class=\"blogBlogContainer\" data-number=\"guides\">\n                                \t\n\n        <div class=\"blogCard\">\n            <span class=\"blogSnipImg\"><a href=\"/content/how-to-clean-your-bike.aspx\" onclick=\"ga('send', 'event',  'Homepage' , 'Click', '/content/how-to-clean-your-bike.aspx', {'nonInteraction': 1})\"> <img src=\"https://license.citruslime.com/cs/blogs/rutland/cleanyourbikehero_790FEE0A.jpg?width=400\" width=\"400\"></a></span><span class=\"blogSnipText\">   Keeping your bike clean is essential for component longevity and your own morale. Seeing a spotless bike waiting for you in the shed before heading out for a ride is a great boost, regardless of what the weather is like outside. Clean bikes just feel better to ride, fact...  For those not in the know, cleaning<a href=\"/content/how-to-clean-your-bike.aspx\" onclick=\"ga('send', 'event',  'Homepage' , 'Click', '/content/how-to-clean-your-bike.aspx', {'nonInteraction': 1})\">.... More </a></span>\n            <a href=\"/content/how-to-clean-your-bike.aspx\" class=\"bBottom4\" onclick=\"ga('send', 'event',  'Homepage' , 'Click', '/content/how-to-clean-your-bike.aspx', {'nonInteraction': 1})\"><span class=\"fa\"></span> How to Clean Your Bike</a>\n        </div>\n    \n        <div class=\"blogCard\">\n            <span class=\"blogSnipImg\"><a href=\"/content/folding-bike-guide.aspx\" onclick=\"ga('send', 'event',  'Homepage' , 'Click', '/content/folding-bike-guide.aspx', {'nonInteraction': 1})\"> <img src=\"/images/folding-bike-guide-head-2016.jpg?width=400\" width=\"400\"></a></span><span class=\"blogSnipText\">   What is a Folding Bike?  Folding bikes are a great way of incorporating cycling into your daily life. They are particularly popular for people who live in urban areas and those who might not have the storage space for a normal bike at home because of their compact size and versatility.  Public transport and commuting<a href=\"/content/folding-bike-guide.aspx\" onclick=\"ga('send', 'event',  'Homepage' , 'Click', '/content/folding-bike-guide.aspx', {'nonInteraction': 1})\">.... More </a></span>\n            <a href=\"/content/folding-bike-guide.aspx\" class=\"bBottom4\" onclick=\"ga('send', 'event',  'Homepage' , 'Click', '/content/folding-bike-guide.aspx', {'nonInteraction': 1})\"><span class=\"fa\"></span> Folding Bike Guide</a>\n        </div>\n    \n        <div class=\"blogCard\">\n            <span class=\"blogSnipImg\"><a href=\"/content/touring-bike-guide.aspx\" onclick=\"ga('send', 'event',  'Homepage' , 'Click', '/content/touring-bike-guide.aspx', {'nonInteraction': 1})\"> <img src=\"/Images/touring-bike-guide-head.jpg?width=400\" width=\"400\"></a></span><span class=\"blogSnipText\">  What is a Touring Bike?  Touring bikes are specifically designed to comfortably help carry you and all your luggage on whatever kind of journey you can dream up. They usually resemble road bikes, using 700C wheels and drop handlebars, but will use more relaxed frame geometries and wider tyres to provide the comfort needed for those epic<a href=\"/content/touring-bike-guide.aspx\" onclick=\"ga('send', 'event',  'Homepage' , 'Click', '/content/touring-bike-guide.aspx', {'nonInteraction': 1})\">.... More </a></span>\n            <a href=\"/content/touring-bike-guide.aspx\" class=\"bBottom4\" onclick=\"ga('send', 'event',  'Homepage' , 'Click', '/content/touring-bike-guide.aspx', {'nonInteraction': 1})\"><span class=\"fa\"></span> Touring Bike Guide</a>\n        </div>\n    \n        <div class=\"blogCard\">\n            <span class=\"blogSnipImg\"><a href=\"/content/road-bike-guide.aspx\" onclick=\"ga('send', 'event',  'Homepage' , 'Click', '/content/road-bike-guide.aspx', {'nonInteraction': 1})\"> <img src=\"/Images/road-bike-guide-head.jpg?width=400\" width=\"400\"></a></span><span class=\"blogSnipText\">  What is a Road Bike?  Road bikes (also known as racing bikes) are easy to recognise, with their drop handlebars, 28-inch (700c) wheels and narrow tyres – they’re what the professionals use to conquer the mileage and mountains of races like the Tour de France. The large wheels and thin tyres of a road bike help it<a href=\"/content/road-bike-guide.aspx\" onclick=\"ga('send', 'event',  'Homepage' , 'Click', '/content/road-bike-guide.aspx', {'nonInteraction': 1})\">.... More </a></span>\n            <a href=\"/content/road-bike-guide.aspx\" class=\"bBottom4\" onclick=\"ga('send', 'event',  'Homepage' , 'Click', '/content/road-bike-guide.aspx', {'nonInteraction': 1})\"><span class=\"fa\"></span> Road Bike Guide</a>\n        </div>\n    \n\n                                </div>\n                                <a href=\"/blog/blog.aspx?tag=guides\" class=\"button bSquare btn-thin-border\">All Guides</a>\n                            </div>\n                        </div>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"col-1 ctrPad16 centralise\">\n                \t<h1 class=\"hmWhyBuyTitle\">Rutland Cycling.
